## Key Findings

1. **Governance Capture Risk**: Significant effect (F=214.3, p<0.001). Ranges from 0.2891 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=250_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0) to 0.5209 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=0_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0.3).

2. **Delegate Concentration**: Significant effect (F=163.3, p<0.001). Ranges from 0.2643 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0.2_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=250_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0.3) to 0.4519 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=0_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0.3).

3. **Voting Power Utilization**: Significant effect (F=67.1, p<0.001). Ranges from 0.0723 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0.2_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=250_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0.6) to 0.1394 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0.2_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=0_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0).

4. **Whale Influence**: Significant effect (F=37.7, p<0.001). Ranges from 0.1041 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0.2_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=250_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0.3) to 0.2585 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0.1_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=0_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0).

5. **Quorum Reach Rate**: Significant effect (F=21.3, p<0.001). Ranges from 0.3763 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0.2_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=250_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0.6) to 0.5532 (at Sweep Value=vote_power_cap_fraction=0.1_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=0_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0.6).

6. 4 metrics showed no significant variation across Sweep Value values.

### Statistical Methods

- **Descriptive Statistics:** Mean, median, standard deviation, coefficient of variation
  - **Confidence Intervals:** 95% CI using t-distribution (bootstrap CI reported when available)
- **Omnibus Test:** One-way ANOVA for each metric
- **Post-hoc Comparisons:** Welch's t-test with effect size (Cohen's d)
- **Effect Size Interpretation:**
  - Negligible: |d| < 0.2
  - Small: 0.2 ≤ |d| < 0.5
  - Medium: 0.5 ≤ |d| < 0.8
  - Large: 0.8 ≤ |d| < 1.2
  - Very Large: |d| ≥ 1.2

### Limitations

1. **Simulated Environment:** Results reflect model assumptions, not real DAO behavior
2. **Fixed Parameters:** Only Sweep Value was varied; other parameters held constant
3. **Distribution Assumptions:** Some metrics violate normality assumptions
4. **Model Validity:** See code review for known simulation issues

## Power Analysis

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| Current Runs per Config | 25 |
| Recommended Runs | 63 |
| Current Power | 43.6% |
| Minimum Detectable Effect | d = 0.7920 |

**Interpretation:**
⚠️ Consider increasing sample size to 63 runs per configuration for 80% power to detect medium effects (d = 0.5).

## Recommendations

### Data Quality Improvements

#### Warnings (Should Address)

- **Whale Influence**: High variability (CV=54.8%). Consider more runs or controlled conditions.
- **Collusion Threshold**: Non-symmetric distribution at sweep=vote_power_cap_fraction=0_vote_power_quadratic_threshold=0_vote_power_velocity_penalty=0.3 (mean=0.1293, median=0.1053). Consider bootstrap CI.

### Simulation Improvements

Based on the code review and these results:

1. **Implement Voting Power Snapshots**: Current live-balance voting allows manipulation
2. **Fix Quorum Calculation**: Should check total participation, not just votes-for
3. **Add Seed Reset**: Ensure deterministic reproducibility between runs
4. **Fix Staking Interest**: Compound annually, not per-step
5. **Implement Delegation Chains**: Required for realistic high-quorum scenarios

### Statistical Improvements

1. **Use Bootstrap CI** for non-normal metrics (Treasury, Pass Rate at low quorum)
2. **Report Median** alongside mean for skewed distributions
3. **Consider Log-Transform** for treasury analysis
4. **Run Multiple Seeds** and report aggregated results
